--文件: dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f.script
--内容: 
-- DWS sql 
-- ******************************************************************** --
-- author: jh_maokaile
-- create time: 2024/03/06 14:25:42 GMT+08:00
-- ******************************************************************** --
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f (
  compid VARCHAR  NOT NULL ,
  rptid VARCHAR  NOT NULL ,
  rptrevision VARCHAR  NOT NULL ,
  computebatchno VARCHAR  NOT NULL ,
  acctperiod VARCHAR  NOT NULL ,
  cellcode VARCHAR  NOT NULL ,
  cellformula VARCHAR ,
  cellvalue VARCHAR ,
  cellvaluetype VARCHAR ,
  status VARCHAR ,
  ext_src_sys_id VARCHAR ,
  ext_etl_dt TIMESTAMP 

) WITH (ORIENTATION = COLUMN) DISTRIBUTE BY HASH(compid,rptid,rptrevision,computebatchno,acctperiod,cellcode);
COMMENT ON TABLE dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f IS '无';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f.compid IS '公司代码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f.rptid IS '报表代号';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f.rptrevision IS '报表版次';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f.computebatchno IS '计算批次';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f.acctperiod IS '会计期间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f.cellcode IS '单元格代码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f.cellformula IS '单元格公式';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f.cellvalue IS '单元格值';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f.cellvaluetype IS '单元格值类型';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f.status IS '状态';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f.ext_src_sys_id IS '源系统';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacellvalue_jc_f.ext_etl_dt IS 'ETL时间';

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacp_jc_f (
  pcompid VARCHAR  NOT NULL ,
  compid VARCHAR  NOT NULL ,
  compname VARCHAR ,
  englname VARCHAR ,
  compshortname VARCHAR ,
  crcy VARCHAR ,
  postingmark VARCHAR ,
  taxno VARCHAR ,
  idno VARCHAR ,
  startacctperiod VARCHAR ,
  yeartype VARCHAR ,
  acctgroup1 VARCHAR ,
  acctgroup2 VARCHAR ,
  acctgroup3 VARCHAR ,
  groupcompid VARCHAR ,
  ext_src_sys_id VARCHAR ,
  ext_etl_dt TIMESTAMP 

) WITH (ORIENTATION = COLUMN) DISTRIBUTE BY hash(compid,pcompid);
COMMENT ON TABLE dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacp_jc_f IS '无';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacp_jc_f.pcompid IS '母帐套别代码';

COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaacp_jc_f.postingmark IS '记帐时点';

  date_id VARCHAR COMMENT '年月',
  costcenter VARCHAR COMMENT '产线',
  QTY DECIMAL(13,6) COMMENT '战略运营部月度实际产量',
  rdefa VARCHAR COMMENT '备用字段a',
  rdefb VARCHAR COMMENT '备用字段b',
  rdefc DECIMAL(13,6) COMMENT '备用字段c',
  rdefd DECIMAL(13,6) COMMENT '备用字段d',
  rdeff DECIMAL(13,6) COMMENT '备用字段f'
)WITH (ORIENTATION = COLUMN) distribute by hash(date_id,costcenter);

-- ******************************************************************** --
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS fina.dwr_fin_tbzxfhbcbfour_jc_f;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS fina.dwr_fin_tbzxfhbcbfour_jc_f(
        yyyymm VARCHAR  COMMENT '年月',
        factory VARCHAR COMMENT '分厂',
		item VARCHAR  COMMENT '项目',
		itemflag VARCHAR  COMMENT '项目标记',
		standard VARCHAR  COMMENT '指标',
		yearamt DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '年度预算' ,
		monthamt VARCHAR  COMMENT '月份预算' ,
		oneamt DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '一月预算' ,
		twoamt DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '二月预算' ,
		threeamt DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '三月预算' ,
		fouramt DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '四月预算' ,
		fiveamt DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '五月预算' ,
		sixamt DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '六月预算' ,
		sevenamt DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '七月预算' ,
		eightamt DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '八月预算' ,
		nineamt DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '九月预算' ,
		tenamt DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '十月预算' ,
		elevenamt DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '十一月预算' ,
		twelveamt DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '十二月预算' ,
		refnog VARCHAR COMMENT '预留',
		refnoa VARCHAR  COMMENT '预留字段A',
		refnob DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '预留字段B' ,
		refnoc VARCHAR  COMMENT '预留字段C',
		refnod DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '预留字段D',
		refnoe VARCHAR  COMMENT '预留字段E',
		refnof DECIMAL (17,4)  COMMENT '预留字段F' 
)WITH (ORIENTATION = COLUMN) distribute by hash(yyyymm,item,factory,standard);
COMMENT ON TABLE fina.dwr_fin_tbzxfhbcbfour_jc_f IS '环保成本4层'

 create table if not exists dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaa03_jc_f (
compid VARCHAR comment '帐套别代码',

acctcode16 VARCHAR comment '会计科目1到7位',
acctcode79 VARCHAR comment '会计科目8到10位',
bgnamt DECIMAL(18,4) comment '期初余额',
dramt DECIMAL(18,4) comment '借方余额',
cramt DECIMAL(18,4) comment '贷方余额',
bgnqty DECIMAL(18,4) comment '期初数量',
drqty DECIMAL(18,4) comment '借方数量',
crqty DECIMAL(18,4) comment '贷方数量',
bgncrcyamt DECIMAL(18,4) comment '外币期初余额',
drcrcyamt DECIMAL(18,4) comment '外币借方余额',
crcrcyamt DECIMAL(18,4) comment '外币贷方余额',
ext_etl_dt timestamp COMMENT 'ETL时间',

)WITH (ORIENTATION = COLUMN) distribute by hash(compid, acctcode, idcode, acctperiod);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS  dwr_fin.dwr_fin_t_dim_object_jc_f;

    code VARCHAR,
    type_id VARCHAR,
    description VARCHAR,
    is_leaf VARCHAR,
    object_id VARCHAR,
    update_date TIMESTAMP,
    path VARCHAR,
    depth VARCHAR,
    parent_id VARCHAR,
    name VARCHAR,
    position VARCHAR,
    create_date TIMESTAMP,
    status VARCHAR,
    ext_src_sys_id varchar,
    ext_etl_dt TIMESTAMP
) WITH (ORIENTATION = COLUMN);
COMMENT ON TABLE dwr_fin.dwr_fin_t_dim_object_jc_f IS '维度成员表';

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS dwr_fin.dwr_fin_t_voucher_main_area_jc_f(

    year VARCHAR,
    operator_id VARCHAR,
    applicant_date TIMESTAMP,
    source_data_row_id VARCHAR,
    reverse_pusher_id VARCHAR,
    pusher_id VARCHAR,
    postor_id VARCHAR,
    pushbmsg VARCHAR,
    bill_type_category VARCHAR,
    push_date TIMESTAMP,
    create_date TIMESTAMP,
    app_id VARCHAR,
    nature_credit_total_amount VARCHAR,
    error_message VARCHAR,
    period VARCHAR,
    nature_debit_total_amount VARCHAR,
    exchange_rate VARCHAR,
    voucher_status VARCHAR,
    version VARCHAR,
    update_date TIMESTAMP,
    voucher_bill_template_id VARCHAR,
    voucher_title VARCHAR,
    creator_id VARCHAR,
    history_status VARCHAR,
    accounting_date TIMESTAMP,
    main_bill_code VARCHAR,
    bill_code VARCHAR,
    voucher_no VARCHAR,
    accounting_subject VARCHAR,
    original_debit_total_amount VARCHAR,
    original_credit_total_amount VARCHAR,
    normal_bill_main_id VARCHAR,
    reverse_date TIMESTAMP,
    bill_type_id VARCHAR,
    bill_type_code VARCHAR,
    voucher_back_reason VARCHAR,
    batch_no VARCHAR,
    bill_main_id VARCHAR,
    casher_id VARCHAR,
    bill_define_id VARCHAR,
    voucher_business_date TIMESTAMP,
    is_balance VARCHAR,
    applicant_id VARCHAR,
    is_pushb VARCHAR,
    is_pusha VARCHAR,
    voucher_type VARCHAR,
    pushamsg VARCHAR,
    bill_type_major VARCHAR,
    bill_define_history_id VARCHAR,
    attach_num VARCHAR,
    currency_id VARCHAR,
    reverse_voucher_no VARCHAR,
    ext_src_sys_id varchar,
    ext_etl_dt TIMESTAMP
) WITH (ORIENTATION = COLUMN);

--文件: dws_dwr_qlt_tbzafrd_jc_f.script
--内容: 
-- DWS sql 
-- ******************************************************************** --
-- author: jh_lihaibo
-- create time: 2023/10/19 15:03:07 GMT+08:00
-- ******************************************************************** --
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS dwr_qlt.dwr_qlt_tbzafrd_jc_f;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS dwr_qlt.dwr_qlt_tbzafrd_jc_f (
    COMPID VARCHAR,
    LEAFID VARCHAR,
    ITEMA VARCHAR,
    ITEMB VARCHAR,
    ITEMC VARCHAR,
    ITEMD VARCHAR,
    ITEME VARCHAR,
    DATAA VARCHAR,
    DATAB VARCHAR,
    DATAC VARCHAR,
    DATAD VARCHAR,
    DATAE VARCHAR,
    DATAF VARCHAR,
    DATAG DECIMAL(10, 4),
    DATASEQ DECIMAL,
    STATUS VARCHAR,
    CREATEID VARCHAR,
    CREATEDATE VARCHAR,
    LASTUPDTID VARCHAR,
    LASTUPDTDATE VARCHAR,
    ext_etl_dt timestamp,
    ext_src_sys_id VARCHAR
 -- PRIMARY KEY(COMPID,LEAFID,ITEMA,ITEMB,ITEMC,ITEMD,ITEME) 
) WITH (ORIENTATION = COLUMN) DISTRIBUTE BY HASH(COMPID,LEAFID,ITEMA,ITEMB,ITEMC,ITEMD,ITEME);



--文件: dws_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.script
--内容: 
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc(
labelno	VARCHAR,
confirmtime	VARCHAR,
invoicedate	VARCHAR,
stockno	VARCHAR,
custno	VARCHAR,
paperno	VARCHAR,
orderno	VARCHAR,
orderitem	VARCHAR,
prodcode	VARCHAR,
labelqty	decimal(13,4),
labelwgt	decimal(13,4),
locno	VARCHAR,
labelthk	decimal(13,4),
labelwdt	decimal(13,4),
labellen	decimal(13,4),
    ext_src_sys_id varchar,
    ext_etl_dt TIMESTAMP
) WITH (ORIENTATION = COLUMN);
COMMENT ON TABLE dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc IS '买断数据';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.labelno	IS	'存货号';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.confirmtime	IS	'出库时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.invoicedate	IS	'开票时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.stockno	IS	'仓库别';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.custno	IS	'客户名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.paperno	IS	'提单号';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.orderno	IS	'订单号';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.orderitem	IS	'订单项次';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.prodcode	IS	'产品形态';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.labelqty	IS	'数量';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.labelwgt	IS	'重量';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.locno	IS	'储位';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.labelthk	IS	'厚';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.labelwdt	IS	'宽';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.labellen	IS	'长';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.ext_src_sys_id IS '源系统';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dm_bpa_fic_buyout_data_jc.ext_etl_dt IS 'ETL时间';

--文件: etl_dwr_fin_tbaciotyped_jc_f.script
--内容: 
-- DWS sql 
-- ******************************************************************** --
-- author: jh_wangweilong
-- create time: 2024/01/31 14:00:06 GMT+08:00
-- ******************************************************************** --
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaciotyped_jc_f (
input varchar
,yyyy varchar 
,wce varchar  
,ext_etl_dt varchar,
ext_src_sys_id varchar
) WITH (ORIENTATION = COLUMN) distribute by hash(yyyy,input,wce);
COMMENT ON TABLE dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaciotyped_jc_f IS '投入工序成本科目明细档';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaciotyped_jc_f.input IS '投入工序';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaciotyped_jc_f.yyyy IS '年度';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaciotyped_jc_f.wce IS '投产追溯逻辑';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaciotyped_jc_f.ext_etl_dt IS 'ETL时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN dwr_fin.dwr_fin_tbaciotyped_jc_f.ext_src_sys_id IS '源系统';
